<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>12.&nbsp;&nbsp;COMMITMENTS AND CONTINGENT LIABILITIES  </B></FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>AIRCRAFT COMMITMENTS  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In 2001, the Company entered commitments to take delivery of 16 Boeing 767-300 aircraft, and took delivery of three in the fourth quarter of 2001. As
of December&nbsp;31, 2001, the Company had commitments for the additional 13 Boeing 767-300 aircraft to be delivered in 2002 and 2003. These aircraft are expected to replace the
Company's DC-10 aircraft. Future payments for the additional 13 Boeing 767-300 aircraft will approximate $25&nbsp;million and $78&nbsp;million in 2002 and 2003,
respectively, and approximately $82.0&nbsp;million per year for the remainder of the lease term. In addition to the delivery of
the Boeing 767-300 aircraft, the Company will take delivery of two Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney spare aircraft engines in September 2002 and one in March 2003. Future commitments for these
engines are approximately $0.9&nbsp;million and $2.1&nbsp;million in 2002 and 2003 and approximately $2.1&nbsp;million per year for the remainder of the lease term. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>F-26</FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<!-- ZEQ.=7,SEQ=64,EFW="2075056",CP="HAWAIIAN AIRLINES, INC.",DN="1",CHK=990529,FOLIO='F-26',FILE='DISK020:[02MOC6.02MOC1156]FK1156B.;7',USER='PHENTGE',CD='30-MAR-2002;04:33' -->
<A NAME="page_fk1156_1_27"> </A>
<BR>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>LITIGATION AND CONTINGENCIES  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;From time to time, the Company is subject to legal proceedings arising in the normal course of its operations. Management does not anticipate that the disposition
of such proceedings would have a material effect upon the Company's financial statements. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>LOS ANGELES AIRPORT OPERATING TERMINAL  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On December&nbsp;1, 1985, the Company entered into an interline agreement with other airlines, which agreement was amended and restated as of
September&nbsp;1, 1989 for, among other things, the sharing of costs, expenses and certain liabilities related to the acquisition, construction and renovation of certain passenger terminal
facilities at the Los Angeles International Airport ("Facilities"). Current tenants and participating members of LAX Two Corporation (the "Corporation"), a mutual benefit corporation, are jointly and
severally obligated to pay their share of debt service payments related to Facilities Sublease Revenue Bonds issued to finance the acquisition, construction and renovation of the Facilities which
totaled $111.9&nbsp;million at completion. The Corporation leases the Facilities from the Regional Airports Improvement Corporation under a lease agreement. In addition, the Corporation is also
obligated to make annual payments to the city of Los Angeles for charges related to its terminal ground rental. All leases of the Corporation are accounted for as operating leases with related future
commitments as of December&nbsp;31, 2001 amounting to approximately $215.3&nbsp;million. Rent expense relating to these operating leases totaled $4.1&nbsp;million, $5.6&nbsp;million, and
$4.7&nbsp;million in 2001, 2000, and 1999, respectively. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Member
airlines pay the expenses associated with the Facilities on a prorata share basis calculated primarily upon their respective numbers of passengers utilizing the Facilities. The
Company accounts for its obligation under this agreement as an operating lease and incurred $800,000, $1,068,000, and $605,000 of rent expense in 2001, 2000, and 1999, respectively. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>UNION CONTRACT NEGOTIATIONS  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The majority of Hawaiian's employees are covered by labor agreements with the International Association of Machinists and Aerospace Workers (AFL-CIO),
the Air Line Pilots Association
International, the Association of Flight Attendants, the Transport Workers Union and the Employees of the Communications Section. All contracts, other than the contract with the seven-member Employees
of the Communications Section, were renegotiated in 2001 and Hawaiian is currently in direct negotiations with the Employees of the Communications Section. If an agreement is not reached in direct
negotiations, federally-mandated mediation will occur and could last for an unspecified period of time. Although the overwhelming majority of labor negotiations in the airline industry are resolved in
mediation, there can be no assurance that the discussions will result in an agreement and ratification. The time required to negotiate a contract under the Railway Labor Act varies. Therefore,
management cannot currently estimate the time frame or results of these negotiations. Should Hawaiian and the Employees of the Communications Section be unable to reach an agreement, the Company could
be adversely affected. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>13.&nbsp;&nbsp;RELATED PARTY TRANSACTIONS  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;From July&nbsp;17, 2000 through February&nbsp;28, 2001, William F. Loftus served as Executive Vice President, Chief Financial Officer and Treasurer of the
Company. During this period, the Company paid Mr.&nbsp;Loftus a base salary of $152,000. During this same period, the Company paid The Loftus Group, a financial and management consulting firm of
which more than ten percent (10%) is owned by Mr.&nbsp;Loftus, $638,535 in fees for financial consulting services, plus expenses. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Since
May&nbsp;19, 2000, the Company has invested $3.0&nbsp;million in certificates of deposit with Liberty Bank, SSB, of Austin, Texas. Liberty Bank is majority owned by John W.
Adams and another individual. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>F-27</FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<!-- ZEQ.=8,SEQ=65,EFW="2075056",CP="HAWAIIAN AIRLINES, INC.",DN="1",CHK=921770,FOLIO='F-27',FILE='DISK020:[02MOC6.02MOC1156]FK1156B.;7',USER='PHENTGE',CD='30-MAR-2002;04:33' -->
<A NAME="page_fk1156_1_28"> </A>
<BR>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>
John W. Adams is an employee of the Company, Chairman of the Company's board of directors and the sole shareholder of AIP General Partner,&nbsp;Inc., the general partner of Airline Investors
Partnership, L.P., which is the majority shareholder of the Company. Current directors of the Company include Edward Z. Safady and Thomas J. Trzanowski, both of whom are also employees and/or
directors of Liberty Bank, SSB. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On
December&nbsp;19, 2001, the Company executed an Advisory Services Agreement with Smith Management LLC and John W. Adams, pursuant to which the Company or its successor will pay,
upon the completion of the proposed merger, $4&nbsp;million in cash to John W. Adams and $1&nbsp;million in cash, one million shares of Holdco common stock and Holdco notes with an aggregate
principal amount of $2&nbsp;million to Smith Management. The Advisory Services Agreement provides that it will be terminated automatically upon the formal termination of the Merger Agreement.
John&nbsp;W. Adams is an affiliate of Smith Management. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>14.&nbsp;&nbsp;CONCENTRATION OF BUSINESS RISK  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company's scheduled service operations are primarily focused on providing air transportation service to, from, or throughout the Hawaiian Islands. Therefore,
the Company's operations, including its ability to collect its outstanding receivables, are significantly affected by economic conditions in the State of Hawaii and by other factors affecting the
level of tourism in Hawaii. In 2001 and 2000, one particular Hawaii-based wholesaler constituted approximately 21% and 17% of the Company's total operating revenues, respectively. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>15.&nbsp;&nbsp;SEGMENT INFORMATION  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company operates as a matrix form of organization and offers only one service (i.e.,&nbsp;air transportation), resulting in management concluding that it
operates one industry segment. The Company's principal line of business, the scheduled and chartered transportation of passengers, constitutes more than 90% of its operating revenues. The following
table delineates scheduled and chartered passenger revenue of the Company, in thousands: </FONT></P>

<!-- User-specified TAGGED TABLE -->
<DIV ALIGN="CENTER"><TABLE WIDTH="75%" BORDER=0 CELLSPACING=0 CELLPADDING=0>

<TH WIDTH="3%"><FONT SIZE=1>&nbsp;</FONT></TH>
<TH COLSPAN=2 ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=1><B>2001</B></FONT><HR NOSHADE></TH>
<TH WIDTH="3%"><FONT SIZE=1>&nbsp;</FONT></TH>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>16.&nbsp;&nbsp;SUBSEQUENT EVENTS  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On December&nbsp;19, 2001, the Company entered into an Agreement and Plan of Merger (the "Merger Agreement") among the Company, Aloha Airgroup,&nbsp;Inc.
("Aloha"), TurnWorks Acquisition III,&nbsp;Inc. ("Holdco") and TurnWorks,&nbsp;Inc. ("TurnWorks"), pursuant to which each of the Company and Aloha has agreed to become a wholly owned subsidiary of
Holdco and the existing shareholders of the Company and Aloha would become, along with TurnWorks, shareholders of Holdco (the "proposed merger"). On February&nbsp;14, 2002, Holdco and its
subsidiaries filed a Registration Statement on Form&nbsp;S-4 with the Securities and Exchange Commission with respect to the proposed merger. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;When
it became clear to the parties that the April&nbsp;18, 2002 outside date agreed to by the parties in the Merger Agreement would not be satisfied due to the expected timing of
regulatory approvals and reviews and other matters, TurnWorks requested that the Company extend the outside date. After considering the request, the Company announced on March&nbsp;16, 2002 that it
had determined not to </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>F-28</FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<!-- ZEQ.=9,SEQ=66,EFW="2075056",CP="HAWAIIAN AIRLINES, INC.",DN="1",CHK=222806,FOLIO='F-28',FILE='DISK020:[02MOC6.02MOC1156]FK1156B.;7',USER='PHENTGE',CD='30-MAR-2002;04:33' -->
<A NAME="page_fk1156_1_29"> </A>
<BR>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>
extend the outside date. The parties conducted discussions with respect to potential revisions to the Merger Agreement and a potential formal termination of the Merger Agreement, but no resolution
was reached. As the parties have now publicly announced their intentions to pursue other courses of action, the Company has treated the Merger Agreement as having been effectively terminated. The
Company believes the other parties are taking the same position. In 2001, the Company recognized $3.2&nbsp;million in expenses related to the proposed merger. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In
connection with reviewing the results of the first full year of operating its new revenue accounting system, the Company did an extensive year-end analysis of all activity
and reconciliation of air traffic liability as of December 31, 2001. The results of this analysis showed that ticket spoilage occurred in prior quarters and that additional revenue needed to be
recognized in the first three quarters. At year end, the Company also analyzed its excise taxes and with all data available determined that an additional accrual was necessary. The impact of these
adjustments is shown below: </FONT></P>

<A NAME="toc_ka1156_1"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>PW4060 ENGINE FLEET MANAGEMENT PROGRAM AGREEMENT<BR>  <BR>    BY AND BETWEEN<BR>  <BR>    UNITED TECHNOLOGIES CORPORATION<BR>  <BR>    PRATT&nbsp;&amp; WHITNEY DIVISION<BR>  <BR>    AND<BR>  <BR>    HAWAIIAN AIRLINES,
&nbsp;INC.    <BR>  </B></FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><B>DATED AS OF OCTOBER 5, 2001  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT> <FONT SIZE=1>This document contains proprietary information of United Technologies Corporation, Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney Division ("Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney"). Pratt&nbsp;&amp;
Whitney offers the information contained in this document on the express condition that you shall not disclose or reproduce the information in whole or in part without Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney's express
written consent. Neither receipt nor possession of this document alone, from any source, constitutes Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney's permission. Possessing, using, copying or disclosing this document by
anyone without Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney's express prior written consent may result in criminal and/or civil liability. </FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<!-- ZEQ.=1,SEQ=1,EFW="2075056",CP="HAWAIIAN AIRLINES, INC.",DN="2",CHK=472287,FOLIO='blank',FILE='DISK020:[02MOC6.02MOC1156]KA1156A.;23',USER='PHENTGE',CD='30-MAR-2002;04:34' -->

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="kb1156_pw4060_engine_fleet_management__pw402691"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_kb1156_1"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>PW4060 ENGINE FLEET MANAGEMENT PROGRAM AGREEMENT<BR>  <BR>    FOR<BR>  <BR>    HAWAIIAN AIRLINES,&nbsp;INC.    <BR>  </B></FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;THIS PW4060 ENGINE FLEET MANAGEMENT PROGRAM AGREEMENT dated as of October&nbsp;5, 2001 (this "FMP Agreement") is made by and between United Technologies
Corporation, acting through its Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney Division ("Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney"), a corporation organized and existing under the laws of the state of Delaware, and having an office and place
of business in East Hartford, Connecticut and Hawaiian Airlines,&nbsp;Inc. ("Hawaiian"), a corporation having an office and place of business in Honolulu, Hawaii. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS
Hawaiian wishes to use Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney's PW4060 engine fleet management program services; and </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS
Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney is willing to provide PW4060 engine fleet management program services for FMP Eligible Engines, as defined below, upon the terms set forth in this FMP
Agreement. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PRATT&nbsp;&amp;
WHITNEY AND HAWAIIAN HEREBY AGREE AS FOLLOWS: </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>A.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;DEFINITIONS  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In this FMP Agreement, including the attachments hereto, the capitalized terms herein shall have the respective meanings set out below. Except as otherwise
provided, all references to "Attachments" refer to "Attachments" to this FMP Agreement. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Aircraft"
means the 767 aircraft operated by Hawaiian on which FMP Eligible Engines are initially installed at the entry of such aircraft into the FMP Agreement. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"AOG
Event" occurs at the time that an Aircraft is unavailable for operational service solely because an FMP Eligible Engine installed on such Aircraft is unserviceable and incapable of
continued
operation after Hawaiian has performed reasonable on-wing corrective action and no replacement engine is available. An AOG Event terminates upon correction of the unserviceable condition
or at the time a replacement engine becomes available for operational service, whichever occurs first. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Aviation
Authority" means all or any of the authorities, government departments, committees or agencies which, under the laws of the State of Registration of the relevant Aircraft, may
from time to time (</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>i</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>) have control or supervision of civil aviation in that state; or (</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>ii</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>) have
jurisdiction over the registration, airworthiness or operation of, or other matters relating to an Aircraft. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"AWAS"
means Ansett Worldwide Aviation, USA, Ansett Worldwide Aviation Netherlands, B.V., or, subject to Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney approval, any division, wholly-owned subsidiary, or
affiliate of Ansett Worldwide Aviation, USA. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Buyer
Furnished Equipment" or "BFE" means the aircraft manufacturer-supplied or buyer furnished engine-mounted accessories (typically including such items as integrated drive generator,
quick accessory disconnect adapter, hydraulic pumps, shut-off valve and pressure regulating valve). </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Customized
Engine Maintenance Program" or "CEMP" means the program for off-wing maintenance and engine line maintenance established for Hawaiian in accordance with
Section&nbsp;D(1). </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Delivery
Duty Paid" or "DDP" shall have the meaning set forth in Incoterms 2000, as promulgated by the International Chamber of Commerce. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"ECM"
means engine condition monitoring. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Engine
Flight Hour" or "EFH" means FMP Eligible Engine flight hour. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Engine
Build-up Unit" or "EBU" means the set of engine-mounted hardware required to interface such engine with aircraft systems. These aircraft systems typically include
fuel, hydraulic, pneumatic, fire detection and electrical units. </FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<!-- ZEQ.=1,SEQ=2,EFW="2075056",CP="HAWAIIAN AIRLINES, INC.",DN="2",CHK=666198,FOLIO='blank',FILE='DISK020:[02MOC6.02MOC1156]KB1156A.;3',USER='PHENTGE',CD='30-MAR-2002;04:34' -->
<A NAME="page_kb1156_1_2"> </A>
<BR>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Extreme
Environmental Conditions" means atmospheric conditions typical of a severe environment including but not limited to high temperature or high concentrations of particulates such
as sand, volcanic ash, calcium sulfate or other contaminates. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Ex
works" shall have the meanings set forth in Incoterms 2000. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"FAA"
means the Federal Aviation Administration of the United States of America or any successor agency thereto. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"FMP
Eligible Engines" means the PW4060 engines that are identified in Attachment I and Attachment II. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"FMP
Rate" has the meaning set forth in Section&nbsp;B. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"FMP
Spare Engine" means an engine provided by Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney for use by Hawaiian pursuant to this FMP Agreement. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"FOD"
means foreign object damage. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"General
Lease Agreement" means a lease agreement entered into by and between Pratt&nbsp;&amp;Whitney and Hawaiian for a spare engine in accordance with Section&nbsp;C(1)(b) when an AOG
Event occurs as the result of an "Excluded Cause" set forth in Section&nbsp;C(1)(b)(ii). </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Initial
Refurbishment Visit" means the first Performance Restoration Shop Visit performed on each of the eight (8)&nbsp;engines in Fleet No.1. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Life
Limited Parts" or "LLPs" refer to those FMP Eligible Engine parts defined as such in the Airworthiness Limitation section of the applicable Production Approval Holders manual. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Parts
Manufacturer Approval" or "PMA" means the authority granted to a legal entity by the FAA and described in 14 C.F.R. &sect; 21.303, to produce modification or replacement
parts for sale for installation on type certificated products. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Performance
Restoration Shop Visit" or "PRSV" means the accomplishment of all specified disassembly, cleaning, inspection, repair or replacement of parts as required, restoration of
fits and clearances, reassemble and test tasks for the purpose of attaining a full service interval of parts, modules and engines. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Pratt&nbsp;&amp;
Whitney Facility" means the Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney Cheshire Engine Center. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Production
Approval Holder" or "PAH" means an entity holding a type certificate issued under the authority of the Federal Aviation Regulation, Part&nbsp;21. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Program
Manager" has the meaning set forth in Section&nbsp;D(2)(a). </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Quick
Engine Change" or "QEC" means the components pre-mounted on an FMP Eligible Engine to facilitate an engine change. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Spare
Engine Lease Agreement" means a lease agreement entered into by and between Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney and Hawaiian for FMP Spare Engines in accordance with Section&nbsp;C(1)(b). </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Specific
Conditions" has the meaning set forth in Section&nbsp;B(2). </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"State
of Registration" means the country in which the Aircraft is registered. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"Term"
has the same meaning set forth in Section&nbsp;B. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"UTF"
means UT Finance Corporation, a wholly owned subsidiary of United Technologies Corporation and an affiliate of Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>2</FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<!-- ZEQ.=2,SEQ=3,EFW="2075056",CP="HAWAIIAN AIRLINES, INC.",DN="2",CHK=243457,FOLIO='2',FILE='DISK020:[02MOC6.02MOC1156]KB1156A.;3',USER='PHENTGE',CD='30-MAR-2002;04:34' -->
<A NAME="page_kb1156_1_3"> </A>
<BR>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>B.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;TERM OF FMP AGREEMENT  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney shall provide services under this FMP Agreement for eight (8)&nbsp;used engines leased by Hawaiian from International Leasing Financing
Corporation ("ILFC") which have completed the Initial Refurbishment Visit (the "Fleet No.&nbsp;1"), for six (6)&nbsp;new engines leased by Hawaiian from AWAS (the "Fleet No.&nbsp;2") and for
eighteen (18)&nbsp;new engines leased by Hawaiian from AWAS, Boeing or UTF plus the four (4)&nbsp;new spare engines leased from AWAS (the "Fleet No.&nbsp;3). Each engine in Fleet No.&nbsp;1
will be covered from each engine's delivery until the seventh anniversary of each engine's delivery to Hawaiian Airlines for services described in Section&nbsp;C(1)(b), and each engine in Fleet
No.&nbsp;1 will be covered for services described in Section&nbsp;C(1)(a) following the Initial Refurbishment Visit until the seventh anniversary of each engine's delivery to Hawaiian. For engines
in Fleet No.&nbsp;1, visits which are not Performance Restoration Shop Visits, such services described in Section&nbsp;C(1)(a) will be covered from engine delivery to the seventh anniversary of
each engine's delivery. Fleet No.&nbsp;2 will be covered until the fifteenth anniversary of each engine's delivery to Hawaiian Airlines. Each engine in Fleet No.&nbsp;3 will be covered until the
eighteenth anniversary of each engine's delivery to Hawaiian Airlines. </FONT></P>

<UL>
<DL compact>
<DT style='margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT SIZE=2>1.</FONT></DT><DD><FONT SIZE=2>Pricing

<DT style='margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT SIZE=2>2.</FONT></DT><DD><FONT SIZE=2>The
FMP Rate is predicated on the following specific conditions (the "Specific Conditions"):
<BR><BR></FONT>
<DL compact>
<DT style='margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT SIZE=2>a.</FONT></DT><DD><FONT SIZE=2>operation
and maintenance of the FMP Eligible Engines during the Term in accordance with instructions contained in Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney publications and other appropriate
manufacturer's publications;
<BR><BR></FONT></DD><DT style='margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT SIZE=2>b.</FONT></DT><DD><FONT SIZE=2>Hawaiian
accepting delivery of the firm aircraft and spare engines as described in Attachments I and II;
<BR><BR></FONT></DD><DT style='margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT SIZE=2>c.</FONT></DT><DD><FONT SIZE=2>Hawaiian
operating all FMP Eligible Engines during the Term;
<BR><BR></FONT></DD><DT style='margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT SIZE=2>d.</FONT></DT><DD><FONT SIZE=2>[Intentionally
Omitted]
<BR><BR></FONT></DD><DT style='margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT SIZE=2>e.</FONT></DT><DD><FONT SIZE=2>adoption
of, and compliance with, the CEMP;

<P><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="page_kc1156_1_4"> </A> </FONT></P>

<UL>
<DL compact>
<DT style='margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT SIZE=2>3.</FONT></DT><DD><FONT SIZE=2>Pratt&nbsp;&amp;
Whitney reserves the right to make reasonable future and retroactive adjustments to the FMP Rate if there is a material variation in any of the Specific Conditions or if
the FMP Eligible Engines are subjected to Extreme Environmental Conditions. The adjustment (credit or debit) shall not apply retroactively to more than one (1)&nbsp;year of operation unless
significant additional information becomes available. Any adjusted FMP Rate shall be provided to Hawaiian at least thirty (30)&nbsp;days before its application. Once determined, the adjusted FMP
Rate shall remain in effect until there is another material change in the conditions upon which this FMP Agreement is predicated. </FONT></DD></DL>
</UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>C.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;SERVICES  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney shall provide or arrange to provide the following services to Hawaiian for its FMP Eligible Engines upon the terms set forth in this FMP
Agreement. The services described in Section&nbsp;C(1) are covered by the FMP Rate except as otherwise provided in Section&nbsp;C(2), which describes the services that are not covered by the FMP
Rate. Excluded services set forth in Section&nbsp;C(2) will be invoiced at the rates set forth in Attachment VII with such invoices including only the cost of repair/overhaul that occurs as a result
of excluded causes. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>D.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PARTIES' RESPONSIBILITIES  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Customized
Engine Maintenance Program ("CEMP") </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Pratt&nbsp;&amp;
Whitney shall provide to Hawaiian a CEMP for the FMP Eligible Engines, consistent with Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney's and other PAHs' approved technical data, and shall
incorporate applicable service bulletins and Aviation Authority airworthiness directive requirements. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>5</FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<!-- ZEQ.=2,SEQ=6,EFW="2075056",CP="HAWAIIAN AIRLINES, INC.",DN="2",CHK=618821,FOLIO='5',FILE='DISK020:[02MOC6.02MOC1156]KC1156A.;9',USER='PHENTGE',CD='30-MAR-2002;04:34' -->
<A NAME="page_kc1156_1_6"> </A>
<BR>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
CEMP shall establish maintenance requirements, including those related to the determination of the off-wing maintenance schedule. The CEMP shall be no less rigorous than
the instructions for continued airworthiness of the Aircraft issued by the Aircraft's manufacturer and PAHs of components of the Aircraft and shall comply with all requirements of the Aviation
Authority of the Aircraft, so long as such Aviation Authority imposes aircraft maintenance standards which comport with and are not materially different from those standards imposed by the FAA. The
preparation of line maintenance task cards shall be the responsibility of Hawaiian or its designated line maintenance provider. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Hawaiian
shall review and approve the CEMP and shall incorporate the relevant provisions of the CEMP into its continuous airworthiness maintenance program. Hawaiian shall also obtain any
and all necessary approvals of that program from the Aviation Authority and any other regulatory authority having jurisdiction. During the Term, Hawaiian shall at all times comply with the
requirements of its continuous airworthiness maintenance program utilizing its presently established providers of on-wing line maintenance and Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney's designated
off-wing maintenance facility. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Program
Management </FONT></P>

<UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Program
Manager </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Pratt&nbsp;&amp;
Whitney shall appoint a principal contact person from Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney to be the program manager (the "Program Manager") for Hawaiian under this FMP Agreement. The
Program Manager shall identify Hawaiian's maintenance requirements for FMP Eligible Engines and FMP Spare Engines and schedule engine maintenance in a manner consistent with the CEMP. The Program
Manager shall consult with Hawaiian and give due consideration to Hawaiian's operational requirements when scheduling FMP Eligible Engine removals (including, but not limited to time stagger
removals). The
Program Manager shall also coordinate any additional support required hereunder to assist Hawaiian with troubleshooting and problem resolution. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;b.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Program
Coordinator </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Hawaiian
shall appoint a person at Hawaiian's facility to be the principal point of contact from Hawaiian for this FMP Agreement (the "Program Coordinator"). </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;c.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Engine
Condition Monitoring ("ECM") </FONT></P>

<UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;i.&nbsp;&nbsp;Pratt&nbsp;&amp;
Whitney shall perform ECM of FMP Eligible Engines to identify trends in engine performance. Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney will work with Hawaiian to establish
methods to satisfy requirements for compliance with Hawaiian's ETOPS requirements. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ii.&nbsp;&nbsp;Hawaiian
shall provide data for ECM in accordance with Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney's specified parameters, format and data collection process, no less than twice per week.
If Aircraft are equipped to electronically transmit ECM data, then Hawaiian shall arrange for automatic transmission of such requested ECM data to Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney's ground station i.d. HFDPWCR
via ARINC, SITA or other routing acceptable to Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney. </FONT></P>

</UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;d.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Life
Limited Parts Tracking and Management </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Pratt&nbsp;&amp;
Whitney shall track and manage LLPs with a view to ensuring that the replacement of LLPs is concurrent with scheduled engine maintenance visits. Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney
shall use commercially reasonable efforts to ensure that a FMP Eligible Engine does not require a shop visit solely for the purpose of replacing LLPs. </FONT></P>

</UL>
<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>6</FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="page_ke1156_1_7"> </A> </FONT> <FONT SIZE=2>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Record Keeping </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;While
the FMP Eligible Engines are in its possession, Hawaiian shall maintain records on the accumulated hours and cycles for all LLPs and other serialized parts that Pratt&nbsp;&amp;
Whitney may specify. If requested by Hawaiian, Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney will make accessible its internal hours/cycles tracking model at no charge. As maintenance is performed on each FMP Eligible
Engine over time, detailed records concerning the work performed shall be kept in the following manner: All records of the performance of maintenance tasks that are required by the applicable Aviation
Authority shall be generated and maintained (</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>i</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>) by Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney or its designated maintenance provider in the case of the off-wing
maintenance, and (</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>ii</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>) by Hawaiian in the case of line maintenance. The party generating and maintaining the records shall make such records available to
the other party in order to ensure compliance with the requirements of this FMP Agreement and the applicable Aviation Authority. Records shall be in the English language and shall include FMP Eligible
Engine maintenance records, configuration records, FMP Eligible Engine test cell data and FAA Form&nbsp;337 or other applicable Aviation Authority approved documents. Following each
off-wing maintenance visit, Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney or its designated maintenance provider shall provide a report identifying the service bulletins incorporated during that shop visit. The
CEMP related service bulletins and airworthiness directives will be identified separately on that report. Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney may perform periodic audits to ensure that adequate records are
maintained. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Monthly
Operational Reporting </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;No
later than the fifth calendar day of each month throughout the Term, Hawaiian shall provide the Program Manager with a complete monthly statement of the previous month's flight data
for the FMP Eligible Engines and FMP Spare Engines substantially in the form set forth in Attachment VI (the "Monthly Operational Report"). Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney may perform periodic audits to ensure
the accuracy of such reports. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Licenses,
Registrations, Etc. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Hawaiian
shall obtain, as of the Effective Date, and shall maintain or cause to be maintained, all consents, licenses, approvals, registrations and authorizations required </FONT> <FONT SIZE=2><I>(i)</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> to operate the Aircraft in
compliance with the laws of Hawaiian's jurisdiction of organization and the State of Registration and </FONT> <FONT SIZE=2><I>(ii)</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> for the performance by Hawaiian of its obligations under this FMP Agreement. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>E.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ENGINE TRANSPORTATION  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Hawaiian, or its subcontracted personnel, shall perform the engine change of FMP Eligible Engines and then transport the removed FMP Eligible Engines Ex works to
Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney's Facility (or other facility designated by Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney) within five (5)&nbsp;days. Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney will provide one way return transportation of FMP
Eligible Engines to Hawaiian's facility at no charge to Hawaiian. Risk of loss remains with Hawaiian both ways. </FONT></P>

the event the number of Hawaiian's ready spare engines falls below one (1), Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney will make commercially reasonable efforts to identify a replacement
engine that may be made available to Hawaiian in an expedited manner should Hawaiian need spare engines pursuant to Section&nbsp;F(2). </FONT></P>

the event Hawaiian experiences an AOG Event during the Term which is the result of an Excluded Cause as defined in Section&nbsp;C(1)(b)(ii), Hawaiian shall pay to
Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney the </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="km1156_attachment_iv_united_technolog__att05912"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_km1156_1"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>ATTACHMENT IV<BR>  <BR>    UNITED TECHNOLOGIES CORPORATION<BR>  Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney Division ("Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney")<BR>  <BR>    PW4060 FLEET MANAGEMENT AGREEMENT<BR>  <BR>    TERMS AND CONDITIONS OF SALE    <BR>
 </B></FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="km1156_article_1_#151;definitions"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_km1156_2"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>ARTICLE 1&#151;DEFINITIONS    <BR>  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.1&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>"Buyer"</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> as used herein shall mean the purchaser of Fleet Management Services provided pursuant to this Agreement. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.2&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>"Equipment"</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> as used herein shall mean the Eligible Engines, including related modules, Parts, Components, Engine
Build-up Units ("EBU") and Buyer Furnished Equipment ("BFE"). </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.3&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>"Exchange Part"</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> as used herein shall mean Buyer's parts and line replaceable units which are offered in exchange for
Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney RMS parts defined below, in connection with Off-wing Maintenance. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.4&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>"Operating and Maintenance History"</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> as used herein shall mean all information relative to the Equipment's modification
level, total time, time since overhaul, time since shop repair, the date of removal and reason for removal. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.5&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>"RMS Parts"</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney new or serviceable Rotable Material Service modules and parts which are
exchanged for Buyer's Exchange Parts in connection with Off-wing Maintenance. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.6&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>"SMS Parts"</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean used and new serviceable parts held by Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney for direct sale or for use in
connection with Off-wing Maintenance. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="km1156_article_2_#151;buyer_wa__km101959"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_km1156_3"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>ARTICLE 2&#151;BUYER WARRANTIES OF EQUIPMENT CONDITION    <BR>  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.1&nbsp;&nbsp;Buyer
hereby warrants that, to the best of its knowledge and belief, unless otherwise disclosed in writing before Equipment delivery to Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney, all
articles of Equipment delivered for maintenance services, including Exchange Parts: </FONT></P>

<UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.1.1&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;are
of proper configuration per the Engine Manual; </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.1.2&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;were
produced in compliance with applicable Federal Aviation Regulations and Joint Aviation Requirements; </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.1.3&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;have
not been involved in an accident, subjected to extreme environmental conditions or abnormal operating temperatures, or otherwise operated outside
the limitations of the applicable type certificate as specified in the type certificate holder's engine manual, maintenance manual and other approved technical data; </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.1.4&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;do
not embody repairs or modifications not performed in full compliance with applicable regulatory requirements; and </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.1.5&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;are
repairable at the level of the engine within the type certificate holder's approved technical data. </FONT></P>

</UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.2&nbsp;&nbsp;Buyer
further warrants that, to the best of its knowledge and belief, no Exchange Parts contain component parts not manufactured by the type certificate holder or an
authorized supplier thereof, nor any repairs or modifications not within the type certificate holder's approved technical data and performed by a repair station properly certified and rated by the
United States Federal Aviation Administration. Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney reserves the right to reject Exchange Parts not meeting the criteria described above. </FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<!-- ZEQ.=1,SEQ=17,EFW="2075056",CP="HAWAIIAN AIRLINES, INC.",DN="2",CHK=866001,FOLIO='blank',FILE='DISK020:[02MOC6.02MOC1156]KM1156A.;9',USER='PHENTGE',CD='30-MAR-2002;04:34' -->
<A NAME="page_km1156_1_2"> </A>
<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="km1156_article_3_#151;material_support"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_km1156_4"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>ARTICLE 3&#151;MATERIAL SUPPORT    <BR>  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3.1&nbsp;&nbsp;Under
ordinary conditions, parts removed from Buyer's engines shall be reinstalled in the same engine. If original parts cannot be reinstalled because of repair lead
times, scrap condition, supersedure, or other circumstances, the following material support services will be used by Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney. </FONT></P>

<UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3.1.1&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;New
Parts </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;New
parts may be used to replace scrap, superseded and, in some instances, long lead time repair/modification material. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3.1.2&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Pratt&nbsp;&amp;
Whitney RMS Parts </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Pratt&nbsp;&amp;
Whitney reserves the right to install RMS Parts as required for maintaining engines in accordance with the Buyer's properly approved inspection and maintenance plan. When
RMS Parts are used, and Exchange Parts are accepted by Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney as set forth below, title for title exchanges result and Buyer's repaired Exchange parts are returned to the
Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney RMS inventory. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Buyer's
Exchange Parts shall comply with the requirements of this Agreement, including, without limitation, the Warranties of Equipment Condition stated in Article&nbsp;2 entitled
"Buyer Warranties of Equipment Condition". If, within sixty (60)&nbsp;days of receipt of Buyer's Exchange Parts ("Inspection Period"), Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney rightfully rejects an Exchange Part on
the grounds of noncompliance with such terms, Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney shall at its discretion: </FONT></P>

</UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;require
that Buyer replace the Exchange Part with another repairable Exchange Part conforming to the requirements of this Agreement within thirty (30)&nbsp;days; or </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;scrap
the Exchange Part and invoice Buyer for the price of a new or, if available, a used serviceable replacement part. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Buyer
will reimburse Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney for all labor associated with the subject Exchange Part up until the date that Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney rejects the Exchange Part. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Acceptance
by Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney occurs at the earlier of: </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;notice
by Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney that it has accepted the Exchange Part; or </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the
expiration of the Inspection Period, provided that Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney has not required a replacement part or scrapped the part. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;With

or otherwise that the Equipment is ready for shipment, arrange for shipment of Equipment by a carrier of its own selection to Buyer's place of business or other destination reasonably believed to be

Buyer under Article&nbsp;7, entitled, "Warranties, Remedies and Limitations", shall be exclusive for defects discovered upon inspection. Buyer shall not delay payment pending such inspection. </FONT></P>

<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>ARTICLE 9&#151;TAXES    <BR>  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition to the price for Services and Equipment provided hereunder, any and all taxes (not including any income or excess profit taxes) which may be imposed
by any taxing authority, arising from the sale, delivery or use of Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney's products and for which Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney may be held responsible for collection or payment, either on
its own behalf or that of Buyer, shall be paid by Buyer to Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney. Buyer shall be responsible for any and all interest and penalties relating to nonpayment or late payment of such
taxes due in any jurisdiction. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="ko1156_article_10_#151;material_disposition"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_ko1156_3"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>ARTICLE 10&#151;MATERIAL DISPOSITION    <BR>  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;10.1&nbsp;With
respect to work covered under the Services Rate, Equipment or parts thereof received from Buyer, which in the reasonable opinion of Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney have no
value other than as scrap because they cannot be repaired to a serviceable condition, shall be disposed of by Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney, and no accountability or liability for such parts shall be imposed
on Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney by Buyer. Title to all such Equipment shall vest in Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;10.2&nbsp;With
respect to Excess Work, Equipment or parts thereof received from Buyer, which in the reasonable opinion of Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney have no value other than as scrap
because they cannot be repaired to a serviceable condition, shall be disposed of by Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney, and no accountability or liability for such parts shall be imposed on Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney
by Buyer. Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney agrees, however, to return to Buyer, at Buyer's expense, parts which are either scrap, superseded or uneconomical to repair if so indicated on the face of Buyer's
Purchase Order or supplement thereto. In any event, Buyer's instructions regarding scrap disposition must be received by Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney within thirty (30)&nbsp;days after shipment of an
engine to Buyer or all scrap will be disposed of locally. To assist Buyer in identification of scrap parts returned at its request, such scrap may be shipped in an altered state which will indicate
that it is clearly unfit for service use. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;10.3&nbsp;With
respect to Excess Work, parts for which there are currently no repair procedures and which, in the opinion of Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney, have potential to be repaired
to a serviceable condition sometime in the future, shall be returned, unaltered, to Buyer at Buyer's expense. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><A

<A NAME="toc_ko1156_4"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>ARTICLE 11&#151;LIABILITY LIMITATION    <BR>  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;11.1&nbsp;The
price allocable under this Agreement to any product or service alleged to be the cause, or in any way arising from or related to the cause, of any loss or damage to
Buyer shall be the ceiling limit on Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney's liability, except for the gross negligence or willful misconduct of Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney, whether founded in contract, tort (including
negligence) or strict liability, arising out of or resulting from </FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>(i)</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> this Agreement or the performance or breach thereof, </FONT> <FONT SIZE=2><I>(ii)</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> the design, manufacture,
delivery, sale, overhaul, repair, replacement, or </FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>(iii)</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> the use of any
such product or the furnishing of any such service. In no event shall Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney have any liability for any indirect, incidental, special or consequential damages. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;11.2&nbsp;For
purposes of this Article, the "price allocable" shall be: </FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>(i)</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> in the case of products or services provided under the
Services Rate, Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney's monthly maintenance service charge for the applicable engine, </FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>(ii)</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> in the case of Equipment provided for Buyer's
temporary use under the Equipment Support provisions, Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney's customary daily lease charge, and </FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>(iii)</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> in the case of any other products
or services provided under this Agreement, the price charged by Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney in relation to the product or service alleged to be the cause of loss or damage. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="ko1156_article_12_#151;seller_s_insurance"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_ko1156_5"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>ARTICLE 12&#151;SELLER'S INSURANCE    <BR>  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as otherwise set forth herein, Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney agrees that Buyer's Equipment will, while in the care, custody and control of Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney,
be adequately protected from loss, damage or destruction under the terms of Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney's insurance. Such protection will commence upon Equipment delivery to Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney and will
remain until Equipment is redelivered to Buyer. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="ko1156_article_13_#151;term_and_termination"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_ko1156_6"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>ARTICLE 13&#151;TERM AND TERMINATION    <BR>  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;13.1&nbsp;This
Agreement shall be effective for the term specified. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;13.2&nbsp;Either
party may terminate this Agreement without prejudice to any rights then accrued for material breach upon ninety (90)&nbsp;days written notification to the
other party of such intent to terminate,
provided the notice specifies the cause for termination and such cause remains uncured for ninety (90)&nbsp;days after receipt of the notice. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;13.3&nbsp;With
or without notice, Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney may terminate this Agreement with immediate effect but without prejudice to any rights then accrued in the event Buyer
does not pay within thirty (30)&nbsp;days of the due date any amount payable under this Agreement in the manner in which it is expressed to be payable. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;13.4&nbsp;Upon
early termination of this agreement, if Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney is the non-defaulting party, Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney will re-price previously
provided services covered by the FMP Rate at Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney's then-current standard rates and charges in effect at the time such service was provided and invoice Buyer for any
deficiency in amounts collected to date in respect of such services. If, instead of a deficiency, there is a surplus in the amount collected, Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney will credit this amount to
Hawaiian's account with Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney, provided the aircraft lessor makes no claim to this overage. Hawaiian shall only use this credit to pay for subsequent shop visits on Eligible Engines
at the Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney Facility at Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney's then-current standard rates and charges. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="ko1156_article_14_#151;exclusion_of_benefits"> </A>

requirements specified in this Agreement. </FONT></P>

<!-- ZEQ.=1,SEQ=32,EFW="2075056",CP="HAWAIIAN AIRLINES, INC.",DN="2",CHK=341640,FOLIO='blank',FILE='DISK020:[02MOC6.02MOC1156]KW1156A.;4',USER='PHENTGE',CD='30-MAR-2002;04:34' -->
<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="kw1156_attachment_vii,_appendix_b_pw4__att02490"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_kw1156_3"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>ATTACHMENT VII, APPENDIX B<BR>  <BR>    PW4000 KIT&nbsp;&amp; BIN PARTS FIXED PRICE LISTING    <BR>  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;With the exception of Engine model conversions, the following fixed prices are valid for Kit&nbsp;&amp; Bin parts used to reassemble PW4000 series Engines and
Modules delivered to Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney on or before December&nbsp;31, 2001. These fixed prices will be adjusted annually relative to the Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney Commercial Spare Parts Price List
prices. The adjustment will be based on the percent change in the Pratt&nbsp;&amp; Whitney spare parts prices for the effective year of the adjustment. For the purpose of this Appendix&nbsp;B,
Kit&nbsp;&amp; Bin Parts shall mean those Parts such as O'rings, gaskets, packings, seals, nuts, bolts, washers and external clips and clamps required for reassembly. Prices are based on average
consumption and include minor modifications to Engines or Modules. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Charges
for nuts, bolts, washers, packings, gaskets, and similar Parts that are details of a Part assembly are not included in the Kit&nbsp;&amp; Bin fixed prices listed below and will be
invoiced as applicable. It should be noted that the part number for such a Part might be the same as a Kit&nbsp;&amp; Bin Part used in the final assembly of Engines, Modules and major Engine
assemblies/Build Groups listed below. However, the consumption of these Parts used in the subassembly process have not been included in the prices listed below. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;[Intentionally
Omitted] </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="ky1156_attachment_vii,_appendix_c_in-__att03725"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_ky1156_1"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>ATTACHMENT VII, APPENDIX C<BR>  <BR>    IN-HOUSE MINOR REPAIRS<BR>  <BR>    INCLUDED IN<BR>  <BR>    MAINTENANCE SERVICES FIXED PRICES    <BR>  </B></FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;All of the fixed prices for Engine Maintenance that are provided in Attachments VII include the following minor repairs when such are accomplished at the engine
overhaul facility performing the Maintenance Services on the relevant Equipment (referred to herein as "In-House Minor Repairs"): </FONT></P>

<UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>Welding
(without the need for heat treatment) </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>Blending
(such as blending of fan blades) </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>Shot-peening
</FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>Machining
(as with a lathe) </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>Boring
(as required for bushing replacement) </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>Drilling
(as required for replacement of rivets, removal of seized bolts, stubs, and plugs) </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>Surface
Treating (including painting, graphite varnishing but excluding plating) </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>RTV
replacement (such as on blades and stators) </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>In-situ
repairs (repairs normally done on site) </FONT></P>

</UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;All
other repairs performed at the engine overhaul facility performing the Maintenance Services on the relevant Equipment that are not listed above shall be invoiced at the applicable
Over-and-Above Rates. </FONT></P>
